 [<i>lgr</i>]
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Máhmiloolo áalolo.
 <i>I hope it will happen.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Imaayachitaskaloolo alíilobi.

 <i>Sally expects that I will win.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Akkàamilo akáaloton akkáhmo.
 <i>I didn't expect him to do it but he did.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Aɬchiyalaan áalolo.
 <i>I expect you to go; I do want you to go.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Aɬchiyalaak áalolo.
 <i>I guess you're going.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>

 <i>What do you think about it?</i><font face="Arial">»</font>

 <i>Do you expect me to go?</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Aɬɬalaak achassíihchoⁿ?
 <i>Do you expect me to go?</i><font face="Arial">»</font>

 <i>I wonder (I'm worried about) what's going to happen.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>

 <i>I expect y'all to win.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>

 <i>We expect y'all to win.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>

&nbsp;to break up (of a group)
<br><font size="+2"><b><a name="aamatka"></a>aamatka</b> </font>
<font size="+2">to disperse, scatter, all go home, break up a meeting; to be scrambled (of eggs)</font>
&nbsp;<font color="#800080" size="+1">-LI</font>
&nbsp;(<i>-, aamatilka, aamataska</i>)
&nbsp; [/aamat-ka<sup>1</sup>]
 <i>Var: ahamatka</i>
&nbsp;<font size="0">(DB)</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Lokòokak faykan aamatkat anookati.
 <i>The meeting was over and everyone scattered.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Lokòoliya ahamatko.
 <i>The meeting broke up.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>

 ☞<a href="a.htm#akkáhmi">akkáhmi</a>
<br><font size="+2"><b><a name="akkáhmi"></a>akkáhmi</b> </font>
&nbsp;1.&nbsp;
<font size="+2">to be that kind, be a different kind, to be like that, be something like that; to be together; to do</font>
&nbsp;<font color="#800080" size="+1">-LI</font>
&nbsp;(<i>akkánchi, akkáⁿhili, akkáⁿhachi</i>)
&nbsp; [/akkami]
 [<i>hgr</i>]
 <i>Neg: </i>akkáhko
 <i>Var: akkáami</i>
 <i>Var: akáhmi</i>
 <i>Var: akkàhmi</i>
&nbsp;<font size="0">(DB)</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Choskanin chokaⁿhkan salaklan akkáhmiiyon tankatoomáaɬon ilachiti.

&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>...akkáhchókkota ommitoolo.

&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Akkáamiifan ɬóokat nákson ɬàakat akkáamiyon wíhlit...
 <i>That's the kind, and then too somewhere the kind that has fallen down like that, look for it...</i> <font size="0">(PMB)</font><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Akkáhti.
 <i>It's done.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Akkáhmihchootoha.
 <i>That's the way it used to be.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Akkástóoⁿba.
 <i>It is done repeatedly.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Tikba ostootifòokok ostalbinaachifòokok nàason ichóot nitóot akkàamiimon oìibit ittanowwahchootoolo.
 <i>When they made the fire, when they went and made camp, things like deer or bears, like that is what they'd go together to kill.</i> <font size="0">(NHN)</font><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;2.&nbsp;
<font size="+2">to happen, occur</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Akkáhmitook ommo.
 <i>That's what happened.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Akkáhmimpo.
 <i>That's the way it happened.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Akkáhtik kanohchoolo.
 <i>It's all right.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Akkáhmìi?
 <i>Did it happen?</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Akkáhmihchoⁿ?
 <i>Did it really happen?</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Sàamin akkáhchòmmìi?
 <i>Why did it happen like that?</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Askaíkkofòokayok akkáhtokáhchon ohonkahchoolikha.
 <i>When they couldn't get out, that's what happened, they used to say.</i> <font size="0">(HCW)</font><font face="Arial">»</font>
